Final Summary (AUT):

  • Journal Summary: In Spring 1901, Austria took Serbia with Budapest, shifted Vienna to Budapest, and moved the Trieste fleet to Albania, aiming for Balkan expansion. Russia secured Rumania with its fleet and advanced to Ukraine and Sevastopol, while Turkey occupied Bulgaria and the Black Sea. Italy surprisingly moved Venice to Tyrolia, raising concerns, but also sent its fleet to Ionian Sea, hinting at Balkan interest or western ambitions. Italy initially alarmed me with Tyrolia but then proposed supporting my fleet in Albania into Greece, promising to withdraw Tyrolia in Fall and maintain a DMZ, which I accepted. Russia agreed to a Galicia DMZ and peace in the Balkans but warned against me taking both Serbia and Greece, hinting at opposition if I overreach. Turkey was belligerent, insisting on taking Greece himself and dismissing cooperation, effectively threatening conflict. I pressed Italy to confirm support and withdrawal, which he did, solidifying a temporary Italo-Austrian alliance. Russia remains neutral but wary, while Turkey is openly hostile and uncooperative.
  • Intent: I will proceed with F ALB - GRE supported by Italy's Ionian fleet, aiming to secure Greece. A SER will likely hold or support, while A BUD covers or supports Serbia. I intend to solidify the alliance with Italy by honoring the DMZ and rewarding his support, while preparing diplomatically to coordinate with Russia against Turkey next year. Turkey's aggression makes him my primary target after securing Greece. I will avoid provoking Russia now but keep options open to pivot if Italy betrays or Russia overreaches.

Final Summary (AUT):

  • Journal Summary: In Fall 1901, I secured Greece with support from Serbia, while Italy stabbed me by seizing Trieste with an army from Tyrolia. Germany advanced into Warsaw and Sweden, Turkey took Rumania and Bulgaria, and Russia lost Sevastopol to Turkey but repositioned to Armenia and Ukraine. Builds reflected these gains: I rebuilt an army in Vienna, Italy added units in Venice and Naples, Germany and Turkey both built heavily, and Russia disbanded a fleet in St. Petersburg. I initially pushed Italy to support my reclaiming of Trieste, but he refused, instead proposing moves that favored his own expansion and ultimately dissolved our alliance, threatening Serbia. Russia was cagey, first objecting to my Balkan ambitions, then offering conditional cooperation if I attacked Bulgaria, but refusing to support me into Rumania unless I proved myself. Turkey was openly hostile and dismissive throughout, promising my destruction. England encouraged a united front against Turkey but offered no concrete support. Italy's betrayal and Russia's reluctance leave me isolated, with Turkey aggressive and emboldened.
  • Intent: My immediate goal is to attack Bulgaria with my fleet from Greece to demonstrate commitment against Turkey and potentially dislodge him. I will likely support my army in Serbia to hold or consider a move to Rumania if Russia shows willingness to coordinate. Vienna will attempt to retake Trieste if feasible, but with Italy's betrayal, I may instead defend my core centers. Diplomatically, I will portray myself as the bulwark against Turkish expansion to Russia and the western powers, while preparing to punish Italy for his treachery when the opportunity arises. I will avoid overcommitting to Russia, who remains untrustworthy, but keep lines open for future cooperation.
